<h1 _ngcontent-mve-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="pdfService（PDF服务）"> pdfService（PDF服务） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-mve-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;"> <div><p>本模块为应用提供统一的管理PDF页面的页眉页脚、水印和背景、文档的多种批注风格和书签便捷的PDF能力。</p> <p><strong>注：</strong>涉及到尺寸和坐标的属性都是以点（Points）为单位，一英寸等于72点。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;"><h2 id="section164051883419" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section164051883419" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-mve-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-mve-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">注意事项<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section12475144852610" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>对PDF文件进行编辑操作后，需要调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/pdf-arkts-pdfservice#section660833016157">saveDocument</a>接口将PDF文件保存，确保编辑操作生效。</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;"><h2 id="section1319183318231" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">PdfDocument<i class="anchor-icon <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>由于文档不可同时读写，如果需要覆盖回原文档，请创建临时文档作为过渡。具体请参见下方示例代码。</p> </div></div></div> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">movePage<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section201841723183814" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>movePage(index: number, dest: number): boolean</p> <p>将指定页面移到索引位置。</p> <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"><p>movePage(2, 3)，不会有变化，2是第3页，3是第4页，第3页只能移动到第4页后面，就是第5页，应该是movePage(2, 4)，顺序：0，1，3，2，4。</p> <p>movePage(3, 2)，会有变化，顺序：0，1，3，2，4。</p> <p><span><img originheight="88" originwidth="247" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115239.36841489539441547801961871874592:50001231000000:2800:C86FB4CAA7A6F6976A51464917DEF7FE4F6431BE917D6F4860A820D3360A74A9.jpg" class="notEnlarge" width="247" height="88"></span></p> </div></div></div> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> number, endIndex: number, oddPages: boolean, evenPages: boolean): void</p> <p>插入PDF文档页眉页脚。该方法属于耗时业务，需要遍历每一页去添加页眉页脚，添加页面较多时建议放到线程里去处理。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div width="16.25%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="43.04%"><p>页眉页脚的信息。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>startIndex</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25.6%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="16.25%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="43.04%"><p>起始页，必须大于等于0，0为起始页。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section206080386472" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>addWatermark(info: WatermarkInfo, startIndex: number, endIndex: number, oddPages: boolean, evenPages: boolean): void</p> <p>插入PDF文档水印。该方法属于耗时业务，需要遍历每一页去添加水印，添加页面较多时建议放到线程里去处理。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.1" width="15.110000000000001%"><p><strong>参数名</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.2" width="21.61%"><p><strong>类型</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.3" width="14.49%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.4" width="48.79%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>info</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.61%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/pdf-arkts-pdfservice#section4749820144811">WatermarkInfo</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.49%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.79%"><p>水印的信息。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>startIndex</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.61%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.49%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.79%"><p>起始页，必须大于等于0，0为起始页。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>endIndex</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.61%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.49%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.79%"><p>结束页，小于总页数。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>oddPages</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="21.61%"><p>boolean</p> </td> <td width="48.79%"><p>偶数页是否添加，true表示是，false表示否。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1461px;"><h3 id="section13641714101419" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">addBackground<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" endIndex: number, oddPages: boolean, evenPages: boolean): void</p> <p>插入PDF文档背景。该方法属于耗时业务，需要遍历每一页去添加背景，添加页面较多时建议放到线程里去处理。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.7.1.5.1.1" width="15.110000000000001%"><p><strong>参数名</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.7.1.5.1.2" width="23.23%"><p><strong>类型</strong></p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.7.1.5.1.3" width="14.6%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.7.1.5.1.4" width="47.06%"><p><strong>说明</strong></p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="15.110000000000001%"><p>info</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="23.23%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="14.6%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="47.06%"><p>起始页，必须大于等于0，0为起始页。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 302px;"><h2 id="section113572873718" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet">PdfMatrix<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section113572873718" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>PDF页面的坐标变换矩阵。包含 x, y, width, height,rotate。x, y 指定图像左上角相对于页面的偏移；width, height,相对于原始页面的指定缩放比例；rotate指定旋转角度。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.OfficeService.PDFService.Core</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 531px;"><h3 id="section208235262387" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section208235262387" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3> <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.106.2.1.6.1.1" width="17.07%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.106.2.1.6.1.4" width="11.51%"><p>可选</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.106.2.1.6.1.5" width="42.54%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="17.07%"><p>x</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.43%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.450000000000001%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%"><p>参数名</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.7.1.5.1.2" width="20.580000000000002%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.7.1.5.1.3" width="17.77%"><p>必填</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.7.1.5.1.4" width="36.65%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>matrix</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.580000000000002%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/pdf-arkts-pdfservice#section113572873718">PdfMatrix</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.77%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.65%"><p>坐标变换矩阵，用于在渲染时对页面内容做缩放、平移、旋转等。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>bitmapwidth</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.580000000000002%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.77%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.65%"><p>图片宽度，单位为Points（一英寸等于72Points），取值范围：大于0。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>bitmapHeight</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.580000000000002%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.77%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.65%"><p>图片高度，单位为Points（一英寸等于72Points），取值范围：大于0。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><p>options</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.580000000000002%"><p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/pdf-arkts-pdfservice#section820410147548">PixelOptions</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.77%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.65%"><p>PDF页面转图片参数。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.9.1.3.1.1" width="32.16%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.129.9.1.3.1.2" width="67.84%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="32.16%"><p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a></p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%"><p>当前页PixelMap。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/pdf-error-code">错误码</a>。</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p> </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 414px;"><h3 id="section5592717204016" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5592717204016" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3> <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table><thead><tr><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.151.2.1.6.1.1" width="17.07%"><p>名称</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.151.2.1.6.1.2" width="17.43%"><p>类型</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.151.2.1.6.1.3" width="12.04%"><p>只读</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.151.2.1.6.1.4" width="10.92%"><p>可选</p> </th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.151.2.1.6.1.5" width="42.54%"><p>说明</p> </th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="17.07%"><p>title</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.43%"><p>string</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="12.04%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.92%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.54%"><p>使用一种特殊的语法来表示直接在内容流内的小图像数据。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="17.07%"><p>titleColor</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.43%"><p>number</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="12.04%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.92%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.54%"><p>标题颜色，取值范围0x000000 ~ 0xFFFFFF，默认值：0x000000。</p> <p>(例如：0xFF0000代表蓝色，0x0000FF代表红色)</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="17.07%"><p>isBold</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.43%"><p>boolean</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="12.04%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.92%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.54%"><p>标题是否粗体，true表示是，false表示否</p> <p>，默认值：false。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="17.07%"><p>isItalic</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="17.43%"><p>boolean</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="12.04%"><p>否</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.92%"><p>是</p> </td> <td class="cellrowborder"
